//  ==========================================================================================================================
//
//  AI Profile name:
//
//    Waterwrld (momentary derivative placeholder)
//
//
//  Version: 1.1.5d
//
//
//  Release date: March 5, 2021
//
//  Details about this version:
//
//    a) Recommended for maps with STARTING POSITIONS ISOLATED BY WATER
//
//    b) Does NOT build Kbot nor vehicle combat units.  Builds stationary land based weapons.  Various amphibious units were
//       play tested but abundant ship presence prevents effective AI deployment of some amphibious content.
//
//    c) Does NOT build Escalation AI cheat units ARMCHEAT, ARMUWCHEAT, CORCHEAT, CORUWCHEAT.  However, Escalation v9.5+ have
//       built-in AI economy multipliers of 2x and 4x, respectively, for Medium and Hard difficulty.  Easy is noncheating.
//
//    d) BUILDS LONG RANGE ARTILLERY (land mass permitting) using following limits according to game difficulty setting:
//
//                                             Easy    Medium    Hard
//         Arm Big Bertha / Core Intimidator     0        2        4
//         Arm Vulcan / Core Buzzsaw             0        2        4  <-- Requires optional unit customization (details below)
//         Arm Armageddon / Core Dictator        0        0        1
//
//         The above nonzero artillery values can be exceeded because game engine does not count incomplete buildings when
//         tallying unit quantities throughout game.  That quirk is a consideration in chosen quantities.  Being SeaBattle,
//         starting positions are likely isolated on islands, possibly small ones.  Higher artillery limits within other
//         AI profiles are unable to be used here.  Limited land mass is shared among useful structures.
//
//         AI ability to trigger unit upgrades from Big Bertha / Intimidator to become Vulcan / Buzzsaw requires unit custom-
//         ization via optional addon files.  Basically, unit fbi data file is customized to enable building upgraded version.
//         This AI feature is unavailable within Escalation releases because structures morphing to become other structures
//         have lead to some network data synchronization issues between players during online games.  That issue does not
//         exist during Skirmish.  If you play both Skirmish and online, it is highly recommended having two separate install-
//         ations of Escalation to isolate Skirmish setup from online.  Optional addon AI unit upgrade files are available at:
//           (for Escalation v9.6/9.7)   https://www.tauniverse.com/forum/showpost.php?p=770812&postcount=8
//         Since, Big Bertha / Intimidator units did not change between v9.6 and 9.7, their AI unit upgrade files at above
//         link are also accurate for v9.7.  Additional features within that addon pack allow player to optionally disable
//         AI long range artillery.  Each fbi file defines a specific unit allowing artillery units to be enabled or disabled
//         on an individual basis.  Player can choose to disable artillery unit(s) for only one faction if that is desirable.
//
//    This AI profile is designed for Total Annihilation: Escalation and includes units up to v9.7
//
//  Changes include:
//
//    Since v1.1.5c
//
//    - Adjusted inconsistent submarine, long range artillery progression among difficulty levels
//
//    Since v1.1.4
//
//    - Added and removed unit content changed collectively within Escalation v9.3 through v9.7
//
//    - Added a few units undefined in SeaBattle v1.1.5 (briefly released as v1.2) and v1.1.5b to increase stability and
//      took advantage of the opportunity by slightly boosting tier 3 ocean bound antiaircraft denfense.
//
//    - Boosted torpedo/depthcharge deployment addressing Standby mode stall from submerged nearest enemy (ongoing TA issue)
//
//
//  Standby mode temporary stall:
//
//    An AI controlled mobile combat unit can temporarily stall in Standby mode on water maps when nearest enemy target is
//    not targetable by the combat unit's weapon(s).  Standby mode can linger until non-targetable unit is destroyed or a
//    targetable enemy unit moves closer.  Some examples of naval stall include:
//
//    - mobile land unit fixating on a submerged unit (Wotan and Admiral_94 have improved this within Escalation as of 2021)
//    - certain hovercraft (without depth charge/torpedo) fixating on a submerged unit
//    - submerged amphibious unit (without torpedo) fixating on a floating unit
//    - certain ships (without depth charge/torpedo) fixating on a submerged unit
//    - submarine fixating on a hovercraft unit
//
//    Naval stall has existed in varying degrees since Total Annihilation v3.1c around 1998.  Its frequency increases as
//    amount of submerged units increases.  The following list shows some significant plateaus.
//
//      Total Annhilation Version      Number of Submerged Units
//
//      Total Annihilation v3.1c          5
//      Core Contingency expansion       15
//      Escalation Beta v8.9.0           23
//
//    The naval Standby mode stall is related to game engine's limited handling of AI units.  Its one-track mind causes an AI
//    mobile combat unit to focus on nearest enemy target even when unit's weapon(s) can not deal with the target.  Naval
//    stall frequency would improve if game engine allowed AI unit cycling to second (third, fourth or fifth) nearest target
//    before resorting to Standby mode.  Nonetheless, we must deal with the given situation.  This AI profile has been tuned
//    for submarines to pick up some slack.  Reinforced sub packs will scour the sea floor knocking out submerged targets for
//    surface battles to flow onwards.  Naval Standby mode stall duration has been improved (but not eliminated) compared to
//    some previous versions of Escalation, such as v8.8.0.
//
//
//  Author: TAfan97
//
//    Can be messaged via Total Annihilation Universe forum private messaging at:
//      https://www.tauniverse.com/forum/member.php?u=24519
//    Generally, higher Escalation AI development activity during Canadian winters and often on hiatus outside of those
//    months.  Since number of AI profiles has ballooned to twelve since Escalation v9.2.0, majority of my maintenance
//    updates will involve the more popular AI profiles to maximize benefit from available development time.
//
//  ==========================================================================================================================


// Common section applies to easy/medium/hard

// Following two default weights can be lower but do not fall below 0.02 otherwise Commander stuck in Standby at game start,
// instead, can use Limit 0 for AI to avoid undefined units
Weight ARM 0.2
Weight CORE 0.2
// If there are duplicate nondefault Limit while default Limit exists then TA uses default Limit
// If there are duplicate nondefault Limit while default Limit nonexistent then TA uses first (topmost) Limit
Limit ARM 0
Limit CORE 0

//factories tech 1
//
// Somewhat conservative factory limits are used to set unit flow during early and mid-game stages.  However, during later
// game stage these limits are often significantly exceeded by game engine not counting incomplete buildings when tallying
// unit quantities.  Also, limits appear to be somewhat ignored by game engine during tier 3 stage if metal and energy are
// consistently at healthy levels.
//
// Limit ARMAP 0  // 20191202 Boosted to dedicate some land construction for maps with significant amount of land
// Limit ARMAP 5  // Boosted torpedo/depthcharge aircraft deployment for Standby mode stall caused by submerged nearest enemy

Limit ARMFHP 2
//
// Changed HP after seeing game engine stubbornly not build SY (for that game it was 4th factory) until Game Time 1:03:00
// and another AI (for that game it was 2nd factory) until Game Time 1:13:00 when Weights SY 10, FHP 6, LAB 2, HP 0
// during Hard difficulty with starting Metal 10,000 and Energy 10,000
// Limit ARMHP 0
Limit ARMHP 3
//
// Play tested Limit LAB 1 and Limit ALAB 1 to allow building DECOM (Decoy Commander) to help protect AI Commander.  However,
// game engine gave LAB as first factory more often than low Weight LAB 0.5 should yield.  LAB as first factory was observed
// to give questionable AI game-play.  Detriments included lack of construction on water and Construction Kbot depleting
// Torpedo Launcher placements by building several along shoreline.  On the positive side, Resource Generator limit was
// reached significantly before other AI, giving highest metal output during early/mid-game stage.  Naval production recovery
// was speedy and effective whenever first Shipyard is built.  Further play testing is required to determine repeatability of
// events.  LAB, ALAB and, subsequently, DECOM viability remains questionable.
//

// Play tested Limit LAB 1 and Limit ALAB 1 to allow building DECOM (Decoy Commander) to help protect AI Commander.  However,
// game engine gave LAB as first factory more often than low Weight LAB 0.5 should yield.  LAB as first factory was observed
// to give questionable AI game-play.  Detriments included lack of construction on water and Construction Kbot depleting
// Torpedo Launcher placements by building several along shoreline.  On the positive side, Resource Generator limit was
// reached significantly before other AI, giving highest metal output during early/mid-game stage.  Naval production recovery
// was speedy and effective whenever first Shipyard is built.  Further play testing is required to determine repeatability of
// events.  LAB, ALAB and, subsequently, DECOM viability remains questionable.
//

// attempting to coerce game engine to expedite our first factory.  We could end up with multiple shipyards too early and
// lingering resource drainage.  Mindfully set limit to avoid multiples from becoming a big problem.
// Weight ARMSY 10
Weight ARMSY 13
//

//
// Energy storage guidelines for high energy weapons plus other energy usage.  Possible redundancy for backup on maps with
// both land and water construction.  Overall total for this AI profile primarily spread among ESTOR SES UWES UWCS
// when long range artillery, both land and naval combat:                      250,000 hard / 150,000 medium / 100,000 easy
// when long range artillery, no naval combat:                                 200,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when long range artillery, no mobile land weapons (limited land/artillery): 150,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, has land and naval combat:                    150,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, no naval combat:                              100,000 hard /  50,000 medium /  25,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, no mobile land weapons (limited land):         80,000 hard /  40,000 medium /  20,000 easy
// when land construction unavailable:                                          60,000 hard /  30,000 medium /  15,000 easy
// Plus: Arm needs extra 1 SFUS per 1 FORGE; Arm/Core need 1 SFUS per 5 SHGEN
// Reminder: Any tier-3 Core Vault (no Arm counterpart) each add EnergyStorage 125,000 and MetalStorage 25,000
// Majority of storage preferred underwater because this AI profile tuned for maps with less land mass

//factories tech 1
//
// Somewhat conservative factory limits are used to set unit flow during early and mid-game stages.  However, during later
// game stage these limits are often significantly exceeded by game engine not counting incomplete buildings when tallying
// unit quantities.  Also, limits appear to be somewhat ignored by game engine during tier 3 stage if metal and energy are
// consistently at healthy levels.
//
// Limit ARMAP 0  // 20191202 Boosted to dedicate some land construction for maps with significant amount of land
// Limit ARMAP 5  // Boosted torpedo/depthcharge aircraft deployment for Standby mode stall caused by submerged nearest enemy
Limit ARMAP 2
Limit ARMFHP 2
//
// Changed HP after seeing game engine stubbornly not build SY (for that game it was 4th factory) until Game Time 1:03:00
// and another AI (for that game it was 2nd factory) until Game Time 1:13:00 when Weights SY 10, FHP 6, LAB 2, HP 0
// during Hard difficulty with starting Metal 10,000 and Energy 10,000
// Limit ARMHP 0
Limit ARMHP 3
//
// Play tested Limit LAB 1 and Limit ALAB 1 to allow building DECOM (Decoy Commander) to help protect AI Commander.  However,
// game engine gave LAB as first factory more often than low Weight LAB 0.5 should yield.  LAB as first factory was observed
// to give questionable AI game-play.  Detriments included lack of construction on water and Construction Kbot depleting
// Torpedo Launcher placements by building several along shoreline.  On the positive side, Resource Generator limit was
// reached significantly before other AI, giving highest metal output during early/mid-game stage.  Naval production recovery
// was speedy and effective whenever first Shipyard is built.  Further play testing is required to determine repeatability of
// events.  LAB, ALAB and, subsequently, DECOM viability remains questionable.
//
Limit ARMLAB 1
Limit ARMPLAT 5
// Limit ARMSY 2
Limit ARMSY 5
Limit ARMVP 0

//
// Escalation v8.9.0 CORSFUS_UPGRADE bug observed 20181125 on metal seabed map (Seven Islands map within Totala2.hpi).
// CORSFUS_UPGRADE was seen as the very last standing AI units (2 of them) not yet destroyed and still "under construction"
// on the metal seabed with no associated CORSFUS.  Attacking forces were unable to target them after destroying all other
// units belonging to that AI.  Its location appeared on minimap.  Command "+view" was used to reveal it.  Escalation v9.0.0
// CORSFUS_UPGRADE.bos is identical to v8.9.0.  SFUS_UPGRADE limit 0 (while SFUS.fbi using "Builder=0") allowed 20191114
// play tests to get past 2 consecutive Game Time ~1:00:00 crashes due to:
//   Instruction pointer is 0040BD41
//   ExceptionCode = C0000005 - Access Violation
//   Access violation: Illegal read, data address 0x03307DB0

// reached significantly before other AI, giving highest metal output during early/mid-game stage.  Naval production recovery

// when no long range artillery, no naval combat:                              100,000 hard /  50,000 medium /  25,000 easy

//factories tech 1
//
// Somewhat conservative factory limits are used to set unit flow during early and mid-game stages.  However, during later
// game stage these limits are often significantly exceeded by game engine not counting incomplete buildings when tallying
// unit quantities.  Also, limits appear to be somewhat ignored by game engine during tier 3 stage if metal and energy are
// consistently at healthy levels.
//
// Limit ARMAP 0  // 20191202 Boosted to dedicate some land construction for maps with significant amount of land
// Limit ARMAP 5  // Boosted torpedo/depthcharge aircraft deployment for Standby mode stall caused by submerged nearest enemy
Limit ARMAP 2
Limit ARMFHP 2
//
// Changed HP after seeing game engine stubbornly not build SY (for that game it was 4th factory) until Game Time 1:03:00
// and another AI (for that game it was 2nd factory) until Game Time 1:13:00 when Weights SY 10, FHP 6, LAB 2, HP 0
// during Hard difficulty with starting Metal 10,000 and Energy 10,000
// Limit ARMHP 0
Limit ARMHP 3
//
// Play tested Limit LAB 1 and Limit ALAB 1 to allow building DECOM (Decoy Commander) to help protect AI Commander.  However,
// game engine gave LAB as first factory more often than low Weight LAB 0.5 should yield.  LAB as first factory was observed
// to give questionable AI game-play.  Detriments included lack of construction on water and Construction Kbot depleting
// Torpedo Launcher placements by building several along shoreline.  On the positive side, Resource Generator limit was
// reached significantly before other AI, giving highest metal output during early/mid-game stage.  Naval production recovery
// was speedy and effective whenever first Shipyard is built.  Further play testing is required to determine repeatability of
// events.  LAB, ALAB and, subsequently, DECOM viability remains questionable.
//
Limit ARMLAB 1
Limit ARMPLAT 5
// Limit ARMSY 2
Limit ARMSY 5
Limit ARMVP 0

//
// Energy storage guidelines for high energy weapons plus other energy usage.  Possible redundancy for backup on maps with
// both land and water construction.  Overall total for this AI profile primarily spread among ESTOR SES UWES UWCS
// when long range artillery, both land and naval combat:                      250,000 hard / 150,000 medium / 100,000 easy
// when long range artillery, no naval combat:                                 200,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when long range artillery, no mobile land weapons (limited land/artillery): 150,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, has land and naval combat:                    150,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, no naval combat:                              100,000 hard /  50,000 medium /  25,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, no mobile land weapons (limited land):         80,000 hard /  40,000 medium /  20,000 easy
// when land construction unavailable:                                          60,000 hard /  30,000 medium /  15,000 easy
// Plus: Arm needs extra 1 SFUS per 1 FORGE; Arm/Core need 1 SFUS per 5 SHGEN
// Reminder: Any tier-3 Core Vault (no Arm counterpart) each add EnergyStorage 125,000 and MetalStorage 25,000
// Majority of storage preferred underwater because this AI profile tuned for maps with less land mass
Limit CORESTOR 0

//factories tech 1
//
// Note: Somewhat conservative factory limits are used to set unit flow during early and mid-game stages.  However, during
//       later game stage these limits are often significantly exceeded due to game engine not counting incomplete
//       buildings when tallying unit quantities.  Also, limits appear to be somewhat ignored by game engine during tier-3
//       stage if metal and energy production are consistently at healthy levels.
//
// Limit CORAP 0  // 20191202 Boosted to dedicate some land construction for maps with significant amount of land
// Limit CORAP 10  // Boosted torpedo/depthcharge aircraft deployment for Standby mode stall caused by submerged nearest enemy
Limit CORAP 10
Limit CORFHP 2
//
// Changed HP after seeing game engine stubbornly not build SY (for that game it was 4th factory) until Game Time 1:03:00
// and another AI (for that game it was 2nd factory) until Game Time 1:13:00 when Weights SY 10, FHP 6, LAB 2, HP 0
// during Hard difficulty with starting Metal 10,000 and Energy 10,000
// Limit CORHP 1
Limit CORHP 1
//
// Play tested Limit LAB 1 and Limit ALAB 1 to allow building DECOM (Decoy Commander) to help protect AI Commander.  However,
// game engine gave LAB as first factory more often than low Weight LAB 0.5 should yield.  LAB as first factory was observed
// to give questionable AI game-play.  Detriments included lack of construction on water and Construction Kbot depleting
// Torpedo Launcher placements by building several along shoreline.  On the positive side, Resource Generator limit was
// reached significantly before other AI, giving highest metal output during early/mid-game stage.  Naval production recovery
// was speedy and effective whenever first Shipyard is built.  Further play testing is required to determine repeatability of
// events.  LAB, ALAB and, subsequently, DECOM viability remains questionable.
//
Limit CORLAB 2
Limit CORPLAT 5
// Limit CORSY 2
Limit CORSY 10
Limit CORVP 2

// on the metal seabed with no associated CORSFUS.  Attacking forces were unable to target them after destroying all other

// CORSFUS_UPGRADE.bos is identical to v8.9.0.  SFUS_UPGRADE limit 0 (while SFUS.fbi using "Builder=0") allowed 20191114
